// Grasscutter [Ljava.lang.String;@5cc1bf20 GM Handbook
// Created 2022/08/23 01:10:39

// Commands
       account : Modify user accounts
      announce : Send announcement to all online players, or manage server's announcement
           ban : Ban a player
         clear : Deletes unequipped unlocked items from your inventory. Defaults to 4* level 1 refinement 1 or lower, but can be set higher.
          coop : Forces someone to join the world of others. If no one is targeted, it sends you into co-op mode anyway.
          enka : Copy your character data from official server to private server using Enka.Network service (data taken only from Showcase)
 enter_dungeon : Enter a dungeon
         equip : You can replace current character weapon with a weapon that cannot be used by current character due to different types of weapons.
          give : Gives an item to you or the specified player. Can also give all weapons, avatars and/or materials, and can construct custom artifacts.
          heal : Heal all characters in your current team.
          help : Sends the help message or shows information about a specified command
          kick : Kicks the specified player from the server (WIP)
       killall : Kill all entities
 killCharacter : Kills the players current character
      language : Display or change current language
          list : List online players
    permission : Grants or removes a permission for a user
      position : Get coordinates
         quest : Add or finish quests
        reload : Reload server config
        remote : Use this to access commands from web
    resetConst : Resets the constellation level on your current active character, you will need to relog after using the command to see any changes
resetShopLimit : Reset target player's shop refresh time
      sendMail : Sends mail to the specified user. The usage of this command changes based on its composition state
   sendMessage : Sends a message to a player as the server. If used with no target, sends to all players on the server.
      setConst : Sets constellation level for your current active character
setFetterLevel : Sets your fetter level for your current active character
       setProp : Sets accountwide properties. Things like godmode can be enabled this way, as well as changing things like unlocked abyss floor and battle pass progress.
                    Values for <prop>: godmode | nostamina | unlimitedenergy | abyss | worldlevel | bplevel | switchelement (se)
                    (cont.) see PlayerProperty enum for other possible values, of form PROP_MAX_SPRING_VOLUME -> max_spring_volume
      setStats : Sets fight property for your current active character
                    Values for <stat>: hp | maxhp | def | atk | em | er | crate | cdmg | cdr | heal | heali | shield | defi
                    (cont.) Elemental DMG Bonus: epyro | ecryo | ehydro | egeo | edendro | eelectro | ephys
                    (cont.) Elemental RES: respyro | rescryo | reshydro | resgeo | resdendro | reselectro | resphys
         spawn : Spawns an entity near you
          stop : Stops the server
        talent : Set talent level for your current active character
          team : Modify your team manually.
      teleport : Change the player's position
   teleportAll : Teleports all players in your world to your position
         unban : Unban a player
     unlockall : Unlocks all open states for a player.
       weather : Changes weather ID and climate type. Weather IDs can be found in ./Resources/ExcelBinOutput/WeatherExcelConfigData.json.
                Climate types: sunny, cloudy, rain, thunderstorm, snow, mist
